	OutputLine(NULL, "今日を呼び寄せたあなたの強い意思の前に、…目の前の苦難はもはや苦難ではない。」",
		   NULL, "오늘을 불러들인 당신의 강한 의지 앞에서... 눈앞의 고난은 더 이상 고난이 아니니까.\" ", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(1, 6, "sprite/si1a_wink_a1_", "0", -240, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 8, 200, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>시온</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s13/06/ds41060113", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「…………あんた、お姉の新しい友達ですか？",
		   NULL, "\"당신, 언니의 새로운 친구였죠? ", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s13/06/ds41060114", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "　名前は知らないけど、ありがとう。",
		   NULL, "이름은 모르지만, 고마워요. ", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s13/06/ds41060115", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "…うん、うまく行きそうな気がします。」",
		   NULL, "...응. 잘 될 것 같은 기분이 들어요.\" ", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacterWithFiltering(0, 5, "sprite/ri2_warai_a1_", "2", "maskright", 1, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 9, 300, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#6972c1>梨花</color>", NULL, "<color=#6972c1>리카</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s13/05/ds41050492", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「……うまく行きますですよ。",
		   NULL, "\"......잘 될 겁니다에요. ", Line_WaitForInput);
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 5, "ps3/s13/05/ds41050493", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "オヤシロさまのお墨付きなのです。」",
		   NULL, "오야시로님께서 보증하신 거예요.\" ", GetGlobalFlag(GLinemodeSp));
	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { ClearMessage(); } else { OutputLineAll(NULL, "\n", Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }

	DisableWindow();
	ModDrawCharacter(2, 12, "sprite/ha2a_warai_", "2", 240, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 10, 200, FALSE );
	ModDrawCharacter(1, 6, "sprite/si1a_warai_a1_", "2", -240, 0, 0, FALSE, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 0, 8, 200, TRUE );

	if (GetGlobalFlag(GADVMode)) { OutputLine("<color=#5ec69a>詩音</color>", NULL, "<color=#5ec69a>시온</color>", NULL, Line_ContinueAfterTyping); }
	ModPlayVoiceLS(4, 6, "ps3/s13/06/ds41060116", 128, TRUE);
	OutputLine(NULL, "「はははははははは！」",
		   NULL, "\"하하하하하하하하하!\" ", Line_Normal);
	ClearMessage();

	DrawScene( "white", 1000 );
	FadeOutBGM( 0, 1000, FALSE );
	DrawScene( "black", 1000 );
}
